    1| { Fill in the following sections (removing comment marks ! if necessary),
    2|   and delete those that are unused.}
    3| TITLE 'Rocket 1a'     { the problem identification }
    4| COORDINATES cartesian2  { coordinate system, 1D,2D,3D, etc }
    5| VARIABLES        { system variables }
    6| h(threshold = 0.0001)
    7| v(threshold = 0.0001)
    8| 
    9|  SELECT         { method controls n}
   10| ngrid =1
   11| DEFINITIONS    { parameter definitions }
   12| 
   13| !parameters
   14| 
   15| mfuel1  = 1200
   16| mfuel2 = 1100
   17| 
   18| ! constants
   19| g_earth = 9.80665
   20|  p0 = 101.325e3
   21| t0 = 288.15
   22| L= 0.0065
   23| R_gas = 8.31447
   24| mm = 0.0289644
   25| big_G = 6.67e-11
   26| M_earth = 5.9722e24
   27| R_earth = 6.3781e6
   28| CD = 0.2
   29| A = 1
   30| 
   31| !stage 1 specific constants 
   32| q1 = 2000
   33| v1 = 2500
   34| m_engine = 320
   35| mass_tank = 30*(1+mfuel1/2000)
   36| tfuel1 =  mfuel1/q1
   37| 
   38| 
   39| !stage 2 specific constants 
   40| q2 = 300
   41| v2 = 2800
   42| m_engine2 = 150
   43| mass_tank2 = 15*(1+mfuel2/1000)
   44| tfuel2 = mfuel2/q2 + tfuel1
   45| 
   46| !equations
   47| start_mass = m_engine +m_engine2 +200+mass_tank2 + mass_tank + mfuel1 + mfuel2
   48| m_r_t =   if ( t < tfuel1) then (start_mass - q1*t) else (if  ( t < tfuel2)  then (start_mass - (q1*tfuel1 + q2*t)-m_engine) else start_mass - mfuel1 - mfuel2-m_engine) !mass rocket total
   49| thresh = (L*h)/t0
   50| Tvar = t0 - L*h
   51| expon = (g_earth*mm)/(R_gas*L)
   52| p = if  (thresh < 1) then  p0*(1-(L*h)/t0)^(expon) else 0
   53| rho = p*mm/(R_gas*Tvar)
   54| 
   55| 
   56| ! equations
   57|  
   58| FD = 1/2*rho*CD*A*v^2
   59| FG = (big_G*m_r_t*M_earth)/(R_earth+h)^2
   60| FT = if ( t < tfuel1) then q1*v1 else(if  (t < tfuel2) then q2*v2 else 0)
   61| acc =( FT - (FD +FG))/m_r_t
   62| 
   63| price = 5000*(320+150) + 8000*(mass_tank+ mass_tank2) + 5*(mfuel1 + mfuel2)
   64| 
   65| INITIAL VALUES
   66| 
   67| h = 0
   68| v = 1  
   69| 
   70| EQUATIONS        { PDE's, one for each variable }
   71| h: dt(h) = v
   72| v: dt(v) = acc
   73| 
   74| 
   75| ! CONSTRAINTS    { Integral constraints }
   76| BOUNDARIES       { The domain definition }
   77|   REGION 1       { For each material region }
   78|     START(0,0)   { Walk the domain boundary }
   79|     LINE TO (1,0) TO (1,1) TO (0,1) TO CLOSE
   80| TIME 0 TO tfuel2   { if time dependent }
   81| MONITORS         { show progress }
   82| PLOTS            { save result displays }
   83| for t = 0 by endtime/50 to endtime
   84| history(h) at (0,0)
   85| 
   86| 
   87| 
   88| report price
   89| report h
   90| report v
   91| END
Uorder=3
 H order=3
 V order=3

==========================
SUMMARIZE EQUATIONS
==========================
In the following equation definitions
Derivatives are represented by appending a dot and the differentiated coordinate.
The operator <V> represents volume integration. <Vb> is weighted by basis function.
<Vu> is weighted by the upwind modifer. <Vbu> is weighted by both.
A dotted volume integral represents volume integration weighted by the indicated
derivative of the basis function. 'Beta' represents a basis function.
The operator <S>.c represents surface integration weighted by the indicated
direction cosine.

==========================
SUMMARIZE EQUATIONS
==========================
In the following equation definitions
Derivatives are represented by appending a dot and the differentiated coordinate.
The operator <V> represents volume integration. <Vb> is weighted by basis function.
<Vu> is weighted by the upwind modifer. <Vbu> is weighted by both.
A dotted volume integral represents volume integration weighted by the indicated
derivative of the basis function. 'Beta' represents a basis function.
The operator <S>.c represents surface integration weighted by the indicated
direction cosine.

   48| m_r_t =   if ( t < tfuel1) then (start_mass - q1*t) else (if  ( t < tfuel2)  then (start_mass - (q1*tfuel1 + q2*t)-m_engine) else start_mass - mfuel1 - mfuel2-m_engine) !mass rocket total
   49| thresh = (L*h)/t0
   50| Tvar = t0 - L*h
   51| expon = (g_earth*mm)/(R_gas*L)
   52| p = if  (thresh < 1) then  p0*(1-(L*h)/t0)^(expon) else 0
   53| rho = p*mm/(R_gas*Tvar)
   54| 
   55| 
   56| ! equations
   57|  
   58| FD = 1/2*rho*CD*A*v^2
   59| FG = (big_G*m_r_t*M_earth)/(R_earth+h)^2
   60| FT = if ( t < tfuel1) then q1*v1 else(if  (t < tfuel2) then q2*v2 else 0)
   61| acc =( FT - (FD +FG))/m_r_t
   62| 
   63| price = 5000*(320+150) + 8000*(mass_tank+ mass_tank2) + 5*(mfuel1 + mfuel2)

In the following equation definitions
Derivatives are represented by appending a dot and the differentiated coordinate.
The operator <V> represents volume integration. <Vb> is weighted by basis function.
<Vu> is weighted by the upwind modifer. <Vbu> is weighted by both.
A dotted volume integral represents volume integration weighted by the indicated
derivative of the basis function. 'Beta' represents a basis function.
The operator <S>.c represents surface integration weighted by the indicated
direction cosine.

    1| { Fill in the following sections (removing comment marks ! if necessary),
    2|   and delete those that are unused.}
    3| TITLE 'Rocket 1a'     { the problem identification }
    4| COORDINATES cartesian2  { coordinate system, 1D,2D,3D, etc }
    5| VARIABLES        { system variables }
    6| h(threshold = 0.0001)
    7| v(threshold = 0.0001)
    8| 
    9|  SELECT         { method controls n}
   10| ngrid =1
   11| DEFINITIONS    { parameter definitions }
   12| 
   13| !parameters
   14| 
   15| mfuel1  = 1200
   16| mfuel2 = 1100
   17| 
   18| ! constants
   19| g_earth = 9.80665
   20|  p0 = 101.325e3
   21| t0 = 288.15
   22| L= 0.0065
   23| R_gas = 8.31447
   24| mm = 0.0289644
   25| big_G = 6.67e-11
   26| M_earth = 5.9722e24
   27| R_earth = 6.3781e6
   28| CD = 0.2
   29| A = 1
   30| 
   31| !stage 1 specific constants 
   32| q1 = 2000
   33| v1 = 2500
   34| m_engine = 320
   35| mass_tank = 30*(1+mfuel1/2000)
   36| tfuel1 =  mfuel1/q1
   37| 
   38| 
   39| !stage 2 specific constants 
   40| q2 = 300
   41| v2 = 2800
   42| m_engine2 = 150
   43| mass_tank2 = 15*(1+mfuel2/1000)
   44| tfuel2 = mfuel2/q2 + tfuel1
   45| 
   46| !equations
   47| start_mass = m_engine +m_engine2 +200+mass_tank2 + mass_tank + mfuel1 + mfuel2
   48| m_r_t =   if ( t < tfuel1) then (start_mass - q1*t) else (if  ( t < tfuel2)  then (start_mass - (q1*tfuel1 + q2*t)-m_engine) else start_mass - mfuel1 - mfuel2-m_engine) !mass rocket total
   49| thresh = (L*h)/t0
   50| Tvar = t0 - L*h
   51| expon = (g_earth*mm)/(R_gas*L)
   52| p = if  (thresh < 1) then  p0*(1-(L*h)/t0)^(expon) else 0
   53| rho = p*mm/(R_gas*Tvar)
   54| 
   55| 
   56| ! equations
   57|  
   58| FD = 1/2*rho*CD*A*v^2
   59| FG = (big_G*m_r_t*M_earth)/(R_earth+h)^2
   60| FT = if ( t < tfuel1) then q1*v1 else(if  (t < tfuel2) then q2*v2 else 0)
   61| acc =( FT - (FD +FG))/m_r_t
   62| 
   63| price = 5000*(320+150) + 8000*(mass_tank+ mass_tank2) + 5*(mfuel1 + mfuel2)
   64| 
   65| INITIAL VALUES
   66| 
   67| h = 0
   68| v = 1  
   69| 
   70| EQUATIONS        { PDE's, one for each variable }
   71| h: dt(h) = v
   72| v: dt(v) = acc
   73| 
   74| 
   75| ! CONSTRAINTS    { Integral constraints }
   76| BOUNDARIES       { The domain definition }
   77|   REGION 1       { For each material region }
   78|     START(0,0)   { Walk the domain boundary }
   79|     LINE TO (1,0) TO (1,1) TO (0,1) TO CLOSE
   80| TIME 0 TO tfuel2   { if time dependent }
   81| MONITORS         { show progress }
   82| PLOTS            { save result displays }
   83| for t = 0 by endtime/50 to endtime
   84| history(h) at (0,0)
   85| 
   86| 
   87| 
   88| !report price
   89| !report h
   90| !report v
   91| END

In the following equation definitions
Derivatives are represented by appending a dot and the differentiated coordinate.
The operator <V> represents volume integration. <Vb> is weighted by basis function.
<Vu> is weighted by the upwind modifer. <Vbu> is weighted by both.
A dotted volume integral represents volume integration weighted by the indicated
derivative of the basis function. 'Beta' represents a basis function.
The operator <S>.c represents surface integration weighted by the indicated
direction cosine.

    1| { Fill in the following sections (removing comment marks ! if necessary),
    2|   and delete those that are unused.}
    3| TITLE 'Rocket 1a'     { the problem identification }
    4| COORDINATES cartesian2  { coordinate system, 1D,2D,3D, etc }
    5| VARIABLES        { system variables }
    6| h(threshold = 0.0001)
    7| v(threshold = 0.0001)
    8| 
    9|  SELECT         { method controls n}
   10| ngrid =1
   11| DEFINITIONS    { parameter definitions }
   12| 
   13| !parameters
   14| 
   15| mfuel1  = 1200
   16| mfuel2 = 1100
   17| 
   18| ! constants
   19| g_earth = 9.80665
   20|  p0 = 101.325e3
   21| t0 = 288.15
   22| L= 0.0065
   23| R_gas = 8.31447
   24| mm = 0.0289644
   25| big_G = 6.67e-11
   26| M_earth = 5.9722e24
   27| R_earth = 6.3781e6
   28| CD = 0.2
   29| A = 1
   30| 
   31| !stage 1 specific constants 
   32| q1 = 2000
   33| v1 = 2500
   34| m_engine = 320
   35| mass_tank = 30*(1+mfuel1/2000)
   36| tfuel1 =  mfuel1/q1
   37| 
   38| 
   39| !stage 2 specific constants 
   40| q2 = 300
   41| v2 = 2800
   42| m_engine2 = 150
   43| mass_tank2 = 15*(1+mfuel2/1000)
   44| tfuel2 = mfuel2/q2 + tfuel1
   45| 
   46| !equations
   47| start_mass = m_engine +m_engine2 +200+mass_tank2 + mass_tank + mfuel1 + mfuel2
   48| m_r_t =   if ( t < tfuel1) then (start_mass - q1*t) else (if  ( t < tfuel2)  then (start_mass - (q1*tfuel1 + q2*t)-m_engine) else start_mass - mfuel1 - mfuel2-m_engine) !mass rocket total
   49| thresh = (L*h)/t0
   50| Tvar = t0 - L*h
   51| expon = (g_earth*mm)/(R_gas*L)
   52| p = if  (thresh < 1) then  p0*(1-(L*h)/t0)^(expon) else 0
   53| rho = p*mm/(R_gas*Tvar)
   54| 
   55| 
   56| ! equations
   57|  
   58| FD = 1/2*rho*CD*A*v^2
   59| FG = (big_G*m_r_t*M_earth)/(R_earth+h)^2
   60| FT = if ( t < tfuel1) then q1*v1 else(if  (t < tfuel2) then q2*v2 else 0)
   61| acc =( FT - (FD +FG))/m_r_t
   62| 
   63| price = 5000*(320+150) + 8000*(mass_tank+ mass_tank2) + 5*(mfuel1 + mfuel2)
   64| 
   65| INITIAL VALUES
   66| 
   67| h = 0
   68| v = 1  
   69| 
   70| EQUATIONS        { PDE's, one for each variable }
   71| h: dt(h) = v
   72| v: dt(v) = acc
   73| 
   74| 
   75| ! CONSTRAINTS    { Integral constraints }
   76| BOUNDARIES       { The domain definition }
   77|   REGION 1       { For each material region }
   78|     START(0,0)   { Walk the domain boundary }
   79|     LINE TO (1,0) TO (1,1) TO (0,1) TO CLOSE
   80| TIME 0 TO tfuel2   { if time dependent }
   81| MONITORS         { show progress }
   82| PLOTS            { save result displays }
   83| for t = 0 by endtime/50 to endtime
   84| history(h) at (0,0)
   85| 
   86| 
   87| 
   88| !report price
   89| report val (h,0)

==========================
SUMMARIZE EQUATIONS
==========================
In the following equation definitions
Derivatives are represented by appending a dot and the differentiated coordinate.
The operator <V> represents volume integration. <Vb> is weighted by basis function.
<Vu> is weighted by the upwind modifer. <Vbu> is weighted by both.
A dotted volume integral represents volume integration weighted by the indicated
derivative of the basis function. 'Beta' represents a basis function.
The operator <S>.c represents surface integration weighted by the indicated
direction cosine.

    1| { Fill in the following sections (removing comment marks ! if necessary),
    2|   and delete those that are unused.}
    3| TITLE 'Rocket 1a'     { the problem identification }
    4| COORDINATES cartesian2  { coordinate system, 1D,2D,3D, etc }
    5| VARIABLES        { system variables }
    6| h(threshold = 0.0001)
    7| v(threshold = 0.0001)
    8| 
    9|  SELECT         { method controls n}
   10| ngrid =1
   11| DEFINITIONS    { parameter definitions }
   12| 
   13| !parameters
   14| 
   15| mfuel1  = 1200
   16| mfuel2 = 1100
   17| 
   18| ! constants
   19| g_earth = 9.80665
   20|  p0 = 101.325e3
   21| t0 = 288.15
   22| L= 0.0065
   23| R_gas = 8.31447
   24| mm = 0.0289644
   25| big_G = 6.67e-11
   26| M_earth = 5.9722e24
   27| R_earth = 6.3781e6
   28| CD = 0.2
   29| A = 1
   30| 
   31| !stage 1 specific constants 
   32| q1 = 2000
   33| v1 = 2500
   34| m_engine = 320
   35| mass_tank = 30*(1+mfuel1/2000)
   36| tfuel1 =  mfuel1/q1
   37| 
   38| 
   39| !stage 2 specific constants 
   40| q2 = 300
   41| v2 = 2800
   42| m_engine2 = 150
   43| mass_tank2 = 15*(1+mfuel2/1000)
   44| tfuel2 = mfuel2/q2 + tfuel1
   45| 
   46| !equations
   47| start_mass = m_engine +m_engine2 +200+mass_tank2 + mass_tank + mfuel1 + mfuel2
   48| m_r_t =   if ( t < tfuel1) then (start_mass - q1*t) else (if  ( t < tfuel2)  then (start_mass - (q1*tfuel1 + q2*t)-m_engine) else start_mass - mfuel1 - mfuel2-m_engine) !mass rocket total
   49| thresh = (L*h)/t0
   50| Tvar = t0 - L*h
   51| expon = (g_earth*mm)/(R_gas*L)
   52| p = if  (thresh < 1) then  p0*(1-(L*h)/t0)^(expon) else 0
   53| rho = p*mm/(R_gas*Tvar)
   54| 
   55| 
   56| ! equations
   57|  
   58| FD = 1/2*rho*CD*A*v^2
   59| FG = (big_G*m_r_t*M_earth)/(R_earth+h)^2
   60| FT = if ( t < tfuel1) then q1*v1 else(if  (t < tfuel2) then q2*v2 else 0)
   61| acc =( FT - (FD +FG))/m_r_t
   62| 
   63| price = 5000*(320+150) + 8000*(mass_tank+ mass_tank2) + 5*(mfuel1 + mfuel2)
   64| 
   65| INITIAL VALUES
   66| 
   67| h = 0
   68| v = 1  
   69| 
   70| EQUATIONS        { PDE's, one for each variable }
   71| h: dt(h) = v
   72| v: dt(v) = acc
   73| 
   74| 
   75| ! CONSTRAINTS    { Integral constraints }
   76| BOUNDARIES       { The domain definition }
   77|   REGION 1       { For each material region }
   78|     START(0,0)   { Walk the domain boundary }
   79|     LINE TO (1,0) TO (1,1) TO (0,1) TO CLOSE
   80| TIME 0 TO tfuel2   { if time dependent }
   81| MONITORS         { show progress }
   82| PLOTS            { save result displays }
   83| for t = 0 by endtime/50 to endtime
   84| history(h) at (0,0)
   85| 
   86| 
   87| 
   88| report val (price,0,0)
   89| report val (h,0,0)
   90| report val (v,0,0)
   91| END

In the following equation definitions
Derivatives are represented by appending a dot and the differentiated coordinate.
The operator <V> represents volume integration. <Vb> is weighted by basis function.
<Vu> is weighted by the upwind modifer. <Vbu> is weighted by both.
A dotted volume integral represents volume integration weighted by the indicated
derivative of the basis function. 'Beta' represents a basis function.
The operator <S>.c represents surface integration weighted by the indicated
direction cosine.
